Source Code

This is the source-code for the Apollo 9 Command Module's Guidance Computer. These files were derived originally from the scan from MIT's Dibner Institute's now-discontinued website titled "History of Recent Science and Technology", which in turn was originally created by Gary Neff, though his high-quality scans were unfortunately reduced in legibility when presented online. The markings on the front of the printout imply that it was the original AGC developer Norm Brodeur's copy. A scan by Ron Burkey has superceded it, made from a more-legible copy from the collection of original AGC developer Fred Martin. The source code was transcribed from those images by Ron Burkey. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	ASSEMBLE REVISION 249 OF AGC PROGRAM COLOSSUS BY NASA 2021111-041
	20'35 OCT. 28,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

000002,000002:                                                                                                  #  Copyright:    Public domain.
000003,000003:                                                                                                  #  Filename:     MAIN.agc
000004,000004:                                                                                                  #  Purpose:      Part of the source code for Colossus, build 249.
000005,000005:                                                                                                  #                It is part of the source code for the Command Module's (CM)
000006,000006:                                                                                                  #                Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC), for Apollo 9.
000007,000007:                                                                                                  #  Assembler:    yaYUL
000008,000008:                                                                                                  #  Contact:      Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
000009,000009:                                                                                                  #  Website:      www.ibiblio.org/apollo
000010,000010:                                                                                                  #  Mod history:  04/30/03 RSB.   Created using the Luminary131 file of the 
000011,000011:                                                                                                  #                                same name as a model.
000012,000012:                                                                                                  #                08/02/04 RSB    Resumed Colossus development.
000013,000013:                                                                                                  #                08/22/04 RSB    Filled in all of the page numbers for the
000014,000014:                                                                                                  #                                individual include-files.
000015,000015:                                                                                                  #                2017-01-05 RSB  Page-numbering adjusted to conform to the markings
000016,000016:                                                                                                  #                                on the printed pages, rather than PDF page
000017,000017:                                                                                                  #                                numbers, which are no longer of interest to us.
000018,000018:                                                                                                  #                                However, I haven't yet modified all of the 
000019,000019:                                                                                                  #                                individual files in that manner yet.
000020,000020:                                                                                                  #                2017-01-06 RSB  All of the individual .agc files for the different
000021,000021:                                                                                                  #                                log sections have now had their internal page-numbering
000022,000022:                                                                                                  #                                adjusted to conform to the numbering of the printed 
000023,000023:                                                                                                  #                                pages.
000024,000024:                                                                                                  #                2017-01-20 RSB  Changed GOTOP00H to GOTOPOOH in all *.agc
000025,000025:                                                                                                  #                                files.  There are probably more POO problems
000026,000026:                                                                                                  #                                but those are the only ones I fixed.
000027,000027: 
000028,000028:                                                                                                  #  The contents of the "Colossus249" files, in general, are transcribed 
000029,000029:                                                                                                  #  from a scanned document originally obtained from MIT's website,
000030,000030:                                                                                                  #  http://hrst.mit.edu/hrs/apollo/public/archive/1701.pdf, though this has
000031,000031:                                                                                                  #  been superceded by a different, much-cleaner copy of the same printout 
000032,000032:                                                                                                  #  we received from AGC developer Fred Martin at one of the following sites:
000033,000033: 
000034,000034:                                                                                                  #  Note that the character-set of the line-printer used did not completely
000035,000035:                                                                                                  #  agreed with the one the developers had in mind --- and this is supported by
000036,000036:                                                                                                  #  detailed comparison to printouts of the slightly earlier Colossus 237 program
000037,000037:                                                                                                  #  and the later Comanche 55 program.  I've been told that this was printed on 
000038,000038:                                                                                                  #  a "page printer" as opposed to the normal line printer used for other AGC 
000039,000039:                                                                                                  #  printouts, and that the page printer had a configurable character set that 
000040,000040:                                                                                                  #  must have been configured incorrectly.  I've interpreted various
000041,000041:                                                                                                  #  wacky symbols appearing in the printout as follows:
000042,000042: 
000043,000043:                                                                                                  #        Printed Character               Intended Character
000044,000044:                                                                                                  #        -----------------               ------------------
000045,000045:                                                                                                  #        plus-minus                              <
000046,000046:                                                                                                  #        lower-case Greek alpha                  '
000047,000047:                                                                                                  #        lower-case Greek beta                   "
000048,000048:                                                                                                  #        lower-case Greek delta                  >
000049,000049:                                                                                                  #        lower-case Greek gamma                  |
000050,000050:                                                                                                  #        lower-case Greek pi                     ?
000051,000051:                                                                                                  #        upper-case Greek Sigma                  %
000052,000052:                                                                                                  #        strange lower-case d                    &
000053,000053:                                                                                                  #        integral symbol                         #
000054,000054:                                                                                                  #        '                                       :
000055,000055:                                                                                                  #        :                                       @ 
000056,000056:                                                                                                  #        (discarded)                             _
000057,000057:                                                                                                  #  As far as the underscore character is concerned (_), I will insert it if it appears from
000058,000058:                                                                                                  #  closely-related program versions that it ought to be there, but there won't be anything
000059,000059:                                                                                                  #  in the actual printout that tells me it should be there.
000060,000060: 
000061,000061:                                                                                                  #  Notations on the scanned document read, in part:
000062,000062: 
000063,000063:                                                                                                  #        Assemble revision 249 of AGC program Colossus by NASA
000064,000064:                                                                                                  #        2021111-041.  October 28, 1968.  
000065,000065: 
000066,000066:                                                                                                  #        This AGC program shall also be referred to as
000067,000067:                                                                                                  #                                Colossus 1A
000068,000068: 
000069,000069:                                                                                                  #        Prepared by
000070,000070:                                                                                                  #                        Massachusetts Institute of Technology
000071,000071:                                                                                                  #                        75 Cambridge Parkway
000072,000072:                                                                                                  #                        Cambridge, Massachusetts
000073,000073:                                                                                                  #        under NASA contract NAS 9-4065.
000074,000074: 
000075,000075:                                                                                                  #  Refer directly to the online document mentioned above for further information.
000076,000076:                                                                                                  #  Please report any errors (relative to scans of the Fred Martin version of the 
000077,000077:                                                                                                  #  printout) to info@sandroid.org.
000078,000078: 
000079,000079:                                                                                                  #  This file is a little different from the other Colossus249 files I'm providing, 
000080,000080:                                                                                                  #  in that it doesn't represent anything that appears directly in the original source.  
000081,000081:                                                                                                  #  What I (RSB) have done for organizational purposes is to split the huge monolithic
000082,000082:                                                                                                  #  source code into smaller, more manageable chunks--i.e., into individual source 
000083,000083:                                                                                                  #  files.  Those files are rejoined within this file as "includes".  It just makes
000084,000084:                                                                                                  #  it a little easier to work with.  The code chunks correspond to natural divisions
000085,000085:                                                                                                  #  into sub-programs.  In fact, these divisions are more-or-less specified by
000086,000086:                                                                                                  #  the source code itself.  Refer to the "SUBROUTINE CALLS" at the
000087,000087:                                                                                                  #  very beginning of the file ASSEMBLY_AND_OPERATION_INFORMATION.agc.
000088,000088: 
000089,000089:                                                                                                  #  It may be reasonably asked why tens of thousands of lines of source are joined by
000090,000090:                                                                                                  #  means of inclusion, rather than simply assembling the source files individually and
000091,000091:                                                                                                  #  then linking them to form the executable.  The answer is that the original 
000092,000092:                                                                                                  #  development team had no linker.  The builds were monolithic just like this.
000093,000093:                                                                                                  #  There was a big emphasis on reusability of the code in the original project, 
000094,000094:                                                                                                  #  apparently, but this reusability took the form of inserting your deck of 
000095,000095:                                                                                                  #  punch-cards at the appropriate position in somebody else's deck of punch-cards.
000096,000096:                                                                                                  #  So, indeed, the method of file-inclusion is a very fair representation of the 
000097,000097:                                                                                                  #  methods used in the original development ... with the improvement, of course,
000098,000098:                                                                                                  #  that you no longer have to worry about dropping the card deck.  On the other hand, 
000099,000099:                                                                                                  #  I wasn't there at the time, so I may have no idea what I'm talking about.
